  FVEFTTEMPLATE (Character 100) — EFT File Template EFT File Template Enter the Bank ACH file format. This format will be used for payment
  FVEFTFILELOC (Character 254) — DefaultEFTFileLoca Default EFT File Location Enter the default folder location to which the Electronic Fund Transfer
  FVPREFIX (Character 3) — Prefix Prefix Enter a Prefix if required for BATCH ID format. BATCH ID Format is
  FVNEXTBATCHNO (Character 10) — Next Batch Number Next Batch Number Enter a numeral value. This number will be taken as Batch ID along
  FVSUFFIX (Character 3) — Suffix Suffix Enter a Suffix if required for BATCH ID format. BATCH ID Format is
  FLAUTHREQUIRE (Logica 1) — Authorization Req Authorization Required Check this field if Authorization is required for generation of EFT File

  FCGLACCT (Character 25) — GL ACCOUNT NO Gl Account No Associated W/ This Bank

  FNDISCRATE (Numeric 6) — DISC PCT Line Item Discount Percentage

  FNUNIT (Numeric 16) — UNIT PRICE Unit Price Of This Item (stocking U/M) Unit Cost (undiscounted) of this line item per this invoice[uses

  FVCONVFACT (Numeric 10) — INV UOM PER VEN U/M Inventory U/M Per Vendor U/M Conversion Factor

  FCSHIPKEY (Character 16) — SHIP ITEM KEY Key to Shitem Table If Fcsource=='S', Then this is the shitem.fshipno + shitem.fitemno
  FEUROPRICE (Currency 8) — EURO EXTENDED PRICE Euro Extended Amount
